        <Math mode="display" tex="\displaystyle mc_{P^{-\frac{n-j}{m}}}(x)={{\operatorname{{Res}}}}_{s=\frac{n-j%&#10;}{m}}t_{P^{-s}}(x)=0\qquad\text{if is odd}," text="formulae@(m * c _ (P ^ (- (n - j) / m)) * x = (Res _ (s = (n - j) / m))@(t _ (P ^ (- s))) * x = 0, [if is odd])" xml:id="S0.E13.m1">
